***bismarck.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bismarck.html>bismarck</a> (17238)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Named <a href = vnd.unilang:for.html>for</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a> statesman <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Otto_von_Bismarck" class="extiw" title="w:Otto von Bismarck"><a href = vnd.unilang:otto.html>Otto</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:von.html>von</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bismarck.html>Bismarck</a></a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
